Phishing</a></h5>\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-time\"><time itemprop=\"datePublished\" datetime=\"2017-04-19T09:58:31+00:00\">Apr 19, 2017, 9:58 am</time></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-author\" itemprop=\"creator\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Person\"><a href=\"https://securelist.com/author/mariavergelis/\">Maria Vergelis</a></span>\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t</header>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-col-2 -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/blog/phishing/78101/personalized-spam-and-phishing/\"><p class=\"truncate\">Lately we have been noticing an opposite tendency occurring quite often, wherein fraud becomes personalized and spammers invent new methods to persuade the recipient that the message is addressed personally to him. Thus, in the malicious mailing that we discovered last month, spammers used the actual postal addresses of the recipients in messages to make them seem as credible as possible.</p></a>\n\t\t</div><!-- class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-time\"><time itemprop=\"datePublished\" datetime=\"2017-04-20T08:57:56+00:00\">Apr 20, 2017, 8:57 am</time></span>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-author\" itemprop=\"creator\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Person\"><a href=\"https://securelist.com/author/kaspersky/\">Kaspersky Lab</a></span>\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</header>\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/analysis/publications/78125/exploits-how-great-is-the-threat/\"><p class=\"truncate\">How serious, really, is the danger presented by exploits? The recent leak of an exploit toolset allegedly used by the infamous Equation Group suggests it’s time to revisit that question. Using our own telemetry data and intelligence reports as well as publicly available information, we’ve looked at the top vulnerabilities and applications exploited by attackers.</p></a>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</article>\n</div><!-- .entry-wrap -->\n<div class=\"entry-wrap clear last\">\n\t<article id=\"post-77855\" class=\"entry post-77855 post type-post status-publish href=\"https://securelist.com/analysis/publications/77855/the-mistakes-of-smart-medicine/\" title=\"The Mistakes of Smart Medicine\">The Mistakes of Smart Medicine</a></h3>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-time\"><time itemprop=\"datePublished\" datetime=\"2017-03-30T09:31:43+00:00\">Mar 30, 2017, 9:31 am</time></span>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-author\" itemprop=\"creator\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Person\"><a href=\"https://securelist.com/author/denisma/\">Denis Makrushin</a></span>\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</header>\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/analysis/publications/77855/the-mistakes-of-smart-medicine/\"><p class=\"truncate\">A technological boom in medicine both encouraged medical institutions to use exclusively information systems in processing data and led to the emergence of new types of technological equipment and personal devices that can be used to interact with traditional systems and networks. This means that the threats that are relevant for them can also be relevant for medical systems.</p></a>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</article>\n</div><!-- .entry-wrap -->\n\t\t</div><!-- content-2 -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-time\"><time itemprop=\"datePublished\" datetime=\"2017-04-11T09:59:59+00:00\">Apr 11, 2017, 9:59 am</time></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span href=\"https://securelist.com/author/great/\">GReAT</a></span>\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t</header>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-col-2 -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/blog/research/77990/unraveling-the-lamberts-toolkit/\"><p class=\"truncate\">The Lamberts is a family of sophisticated attack tools that has been used by one or multiple threat actors against high-profile victims since at least 2008. The arsenal includes network-driven backdoors, several generations of modular backdoors, harvesting tools, and wipers.</p></a>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-content -->\n\t</article>\n</div><!-- .entry-wrap attacks</a></h5>\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-time\"><time itemprop=\"datePublished\" datetime=\"2017-04-04T16:08:41+00:00\">Apr 4, 2017, 4:08 pm</time></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-author\" itemprop=\"creator\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Person\"><a href=\"https://securelist.com/author/anton/\">Anton Ivanov</a></span>\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t</header>\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-col-2 -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/blog/sas/77877/ransomware-in-targeted-attacks/\"><p class=\"truncate\">Ransomware’s popularity has attracted the attention of cybercriminal gangs; they use these malicious programs in targeted attacks on large organizations in order to steal money. In late 2016, we detected an increase in the number of attacks, the main goal of which was to launch an encryptor on an organization’s network nodes and servers. </p></a>\n\t\t</div><!-- Landscape for Industrial Automation Systems, H2 2016</a></h3>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-time\"><time itemprop=\"datePublished\" datetime=\"2017-03-28T09:00:34+00:00\">Mar 28, 2017, 9:00 am</time></span>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-author\" itemprop=\"creator\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Person\"><a href=\"https://securelist.com/author/kaspersky/\">Kaspersky Lab</a></span>\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</header>\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/analysis/publications/77842/threat-landscape-for-industrial-automation-systems-h2-2016/\"><p class=\"truncate\">On average, in the second half of 2016 Kaspersky Lab products across the globe blocked attempted attacks on 39.2% of protected computers that Kaspersky Lab ICS CERT classifies as being part of industrial enterprise technology infrastructure.</p></a>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</article>\n</div><!-- .entry-wrap -->\n<div class=\"entry-wrap clear last\">\n\t<article id=\"post-77784\" class=\"entry post-77784 post type-post href=\"https://securelist.com/analysis/publications/77784/the-cost-of-launching-a-ddos-attack/\" title=\"The cost of launching a DDoS attack\">The cost of launching a DDoS attack</a></h3>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-time\"><time itemprop=\"datePublished\" datetime=\"2017-03-23T08:56:41+00:00\">Mar 23, 2017, 8:56 am</time></span>\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"entry-author\" itemprop=\"creator\" itemscope=\"\" itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Person\"><a href=\"https://securelist.com/author/denisma/\">Denis Makrushin</a></span>\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</header>\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/analysis/publications/77784/the-cost-of-launching-a-ddos-attack/\"><p class=\"truncate\">Almost anyone can fall victim to a DDoS attack. They are relatively cheap and easy to organize, and can be highly effective if reliable protection is not in place. Based on analysis of the data obtained from open sources, we managed to find out the current cost of a DDoS attack on the black market. We also established what exactly the cybercriminals behind DDoS attacks offer their customers. </p></a>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</article>\n</div><!-- .entry-wrap -->\n\t\t</div><!-- content-2 -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content clear\" itemprop=\"text\">\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://securelist.com/blog/sas/77883/penquins-moonlit-maze/\"><p class=\"truncate\">Moonlight Maze is the stuff of cyberespionage legend. To say that this historic threat actor is directly related to the modern day Turla would elevate an already formidable modern day attacker to another league altogether.</p></a>\n\t\t</div><!--
